1+ YearsManual TestingWeb ApplicationsAgile
Apply by: 17 Oct 2025

Software Test Engineers / Software Testers

About KOTT Software:

KOTT Software is a globally recognized, ISO 9001:2015-certified company with a strong legacy in enterprise product development and offshore software services since 1997. With a dedicated international clientele, we specialize in delivering robust, client-focused business solutions across diverse industries. We partner with global organizations to enable and accelerate their digital transformation journey, leveraging deep domain expertise and enterprise application capabilities.

Opportunity:

Join us for the opportunity to work on niche US-based domains and industry verticals, collaborate closely with Fortune 100 clients, and contribute in an agile development environment involving technical reviews, quality assurance, and collaborative delivery.

Minimum Experience Requirement:

At least 1+ years of Software Testing experience in a Web application development environment.

Job Responsibilities:

  • Perform manual testing and related activities in a web-based application environment.
  • Work closely in an Agile development team environment and meet release plan schedules and patch management.
  • Develop and implement test plans, test strategy, test cases, and test reports for various testing types, including regression, functional, and performance testing.
  • Record and track defects using a web-based project management tool.
  • Set up and follow procedures for bug/issues/defects.
  • Responsible for testing all software products/projects.
  • May need to work in flexible hours to attend US/Europe client meetings.

Technical / Functional Skills (Must Have):

  • Prior experience in testing Web-based applications / Enterprise level applications and solutions is a plus.
  • Experience in Manual Testing, including writing test cases.
  • Sound knowledge of the Software Testing Life Cycle (STLC), software testing methodologies, and procedures.
  • Ability to identify test scenarios, create test plans, test strategy, and test cases, and execute them.
  • Sound understanding and experience in developing/executing test cases in an application development environment.
  • Knowledge of Quality Assurance/testing life cycle processes is a plus.
  • Minimum of 1+ years of experience in developing AND executing test cases in a client-driven environment.
  • Experience using any bug-tracking tool.

Preferred Skills:

  • Sound knowledge of software testing methodologies and procedures.
  • Hands-on skills in Selenium, JMeter, or UFT automation tools in a live environment is a plus.
  • Ability to write scripts in Java or VB Script is an advantage.
  • Basic SQL concepts and query writing.
  • Good communication and interpersonal skills.
  • Ability to think ‘OUT OF THE BOX’.

Qualification:

B.E./B.Tech./M.C.A./BCA/BSc. with a Diploma in software testing or quality assurance.

Contact Information:

If this opportunity aligns with your career goals, kindly share your updated resume with us at manualtest@kottsoftware.com

  • Develop preliminary solution outlines, scope summaries, and feature mappings.
  • Create draft Business Requirement Documents (BRDs) or Functional Specifications (FSDs) when required.

  • Coordinate with PMs, Product Teams, and Solutions Architects to validate effort, timelines, and scope.

  • Assist in tailoring and preparing demos based on client requirements.
  • Support solution walkthroughs by demonstrating functionality, workflows, or configuration concepts.

  • Work with the Sales & Customer Success Executive to align scope, requirements, and customer expectations.
  • Provide technical input to marketing collateral when showcasing system workflows or configurations.
  • Support design and content teams with diagrams, Figma links, functionality clarifications, or feature visuals.
  • Coordinate early solution feasibility with PMO, developers, and product architects.

  • Prepare structured handover notes for PMO, BA, and delivery teams to begin implementation.
  • Clarify assumptions, workflows, deliverables, and effort during pre-kick-off activities.

Position Overview

We are seeking a proactive and results-driven Solution Validation Analyst to serve as the critical bridge between business needs and technical quality. The ideal candidate will be responsible for defining, analyzing, and validating robust technology solutions, ensuring they not only meet client specifications but also deliver maximum operational effectiveness. This role requires leveraging strong analytical skills and industry knowledge (preferably in the banking and financial markets) to capture requirements, design the optimal solution, and execute comprehensive testing—including test automation—to ensure flawless delivery and successful digital transformation.

Solution Strategy & Business Analysis (Define the Solution) - Lead the requirements gathering process by working with clients to understand, document, and analyse business needs, ensuring alignment with project goals and objectives. - Evaluate and recommend process improvements for client systems (e.g., banking and financial systems) to enhance efficiency and meet regulatory compliance. - Collaborate with the development team to design and implement technology solutions that meet client specifications. - Prepare comprehensive business requirement documents (BRD), functional specifications, user stories, and process flow diagrams. - Serve as the strategic liaison between clients, project teams, and other stakeholders, ensuring clear communication and managing expectations. - Stay updated on trends and regulatory changes in the banking and financial services industry to proactively identify impacts on client projects.

Validation & Quality Assurance (Verify the Solution) - Design and execute comprehensive test planning and test case design, including defining tests for functionalities and performance. - Develop and maintain robust test automation frameworks and perform hands-on automation for frontend, API, and/or database systems. - Utilize automation tools such as Selenium, Appium, Cypress, Serenity BDD, REST API testing, and Cucumber. - Perform various specialized tests, including performance tests (e.g., using Jmeter), usability, and/or security tests. - Design the overall test strategy for a project. - Assist in creating test plans, perform User Acceptance Testing (UAT), and ensure the final product meets established requirements. - Use defect tracking/management tools such as JIRA and work with version control systems (TFS, git).

QA & Technical: - Hands-on experience in test automation. - Intermediate programming experience in one or more of: Java, C#, JavaScript/TypeScript, Python. - Experience in a continuous integration environment (Jenkins/TeamCity, Maven).

Analysis & Methodology: - Strong knowledge of financial and banking operations, systems, and regulatory requirements. - Proficiency in requirements gathering, process mapping, and documentation techniques. - Familiarity with Agile and Iterative SDLCs and project management methodologies (e.g., Agile, Waterfall).

  • Experience with data analysis tools and Business Intelligence (BI) software.
  • Experience with mobile testing, cloud migration testing, or data integrity testing.
  • Certifications such as CBAP or ACP are an advantage.
  • Experience with fintech or regulatory compliance projects is beneficial.

  • Ongoing professional development opportunities.
  • A collaborative and innovative work environment.

Software Developer Intern

Company: Lean Transitions Solutions Location: Basement Floor, Periyar Building, Technopark Phase -1, Trivandrum, 695581 Website: http://www.LeanTransitionSolutions.com Contact Email: careers@ltslean.com Closing Date: 22, Oct 2025 Job Published: 15, Oct 2025

About Lean Transitions Solutions (LTS)

Founded over a decade ago with headquarters in the United Kingdom, Lean Transition Solutions Ltd (LTS) is an ISO 9001:2015 certified company advocating Industry 4.0. LTS delivers Lean Industry 4.0 software solutions and Leadership 4.0 solutions for world-class organizations globally, including Fortune 500 companies. With global locations across India, Germany, Poland, the United States, UAE, Jordan, and Mexico, our dedicated team ensures client requirements are met with bespoke software solutions addressing industrial and manufacturing challenges. We uphold core values of Respect for All, Integrity, Collaboration, Creativity, Inclusiveness, and Empathy.

Internship Role and Responsibilities:

As a Software Developer Intern, you will:

  • Assist in Software Development: Work closely with developers to design, develop, test, and maintain web and mobile applications.
  • Code and Debug: Write clean, efficient, and well-documented code for various applications and systems.
  • Collaborate: Participate in team meetings, code reviews, and brainstorming sessions to contribute ideas and improve software functionality.
  • Support in Testing: Assist the QA team in writing test cases, performing manual testing, and debugging issues to ensure high-quality software releases.
  • Learn & Implement Technologies: Gain exposure to a range of technologies, frameworks, and development tools.
  • Problem Solving: Troubleshoot and resolve software bugs, ensuring the delivery of high-quality applications.
  • Documentation: Assist in creating technical documentation, user guides, and reports for development work.
  • Research and Innovate: Explore new technologies and approaches to improve development processes and software solutions.

Desired Skills & Qualifications:

  • Education: B.Tech (2024 or 2025 passed out).
  • Programming Knowledge: Strong understanding of at least one programming language (e.g., Java, C++, Python, JavaScript).
  • Basic Knowledge of Web Development: Familiarity with HTML, CSS, JavaScript, and frameworks like Laravel, React, Angular, or Node.js is a plus.
  • Database Knowledge: Basic understanding of SQL and relational databases (e.g., MySQL, PostgreSQL) is desirable.
  • Problem-Solving Skills: Strong analytical thinking and the ability to solve complex problems.
  • Team Player: Ability to work collaboratively in a team-oriented environment.
  • Self-Learning: Willingness to learn new technologies and development practices.
  • Good Communication Skills: Ability to communicate technical concepts clearly and effectively.
  • Additional Qualifications: Certifications or prior internship experience in software development will be considered a plus.

Additional Details:

  • Location: Lean transition Solutions, Periyar Building Technopark
  • Duration: 3 months (with the possibility of a permanent job offer based on performance)
  • Type: Paid, interns receive remuneration for their work.
  • Mode: In Office

To Apply: Interested candidates can send their updated resume to careers@ltslean.com with the subject line "Software Developer Intern ".

Junior Devops Engineer

Reizend (P) Ltd
Technopark

Seeking a Junior DevOps Engineer for technical support on overseas projects. Responsibilities include troubleshooting cloud, networking, and DevOps issues in a 24/7 rotational shift environment.

0.5-2 YearsDevOpsCloud PlatformsKubernetes
Apply by: 29 Nov 2025

Junior DevOps Engineer

Company: REIZEND (P) Ltd Address: SBC Module 15, 2nd Floor, Thejaswini Building, Technopark phase 1, Trivandrum, 695581 Website: http://www.reizendretail.in Contact Email: careers@reizend.ai

Job Published: 15, Oct 2025 Closing Date: 29, Nov 2025

Preferred Candidate Locations: Kerala, Tamil Nadu, and Karnataka Work Location: Trivandrum (Work From Office)

Brief Description

We are looking for a proactive and highly skilled Junior DevOps Engineer to provide exceptional technical support to overseas projects, working in rotational shifts to ensure 24/7 availability. This role involves troubleshooting complex issues across cloud platforms, networking, application architectures, and DevOps toolchains. The ideal candidate should be self-motivated, a collaborator, agile, and a continuous learner.

Key Responsibilities

  • Provide technical support and troubleshoot issues related to cloud platforms and services such as Fargate, ECS, DynamoDB, BigQuery, SNS etc.
  • Understand problems by consuming logs and metrics from various sources using services such as CloudWatch, Prometheus, Grafana, Loki, Alert Managers, and Splunk etc.
  • Analyze and resolve networking challenges, including load balancers, API gateways, reverse proxies, ingress controllers, and service-to-service communications.
  • Work on issues related to client-server communications, firewalls, and virtual machines.
  • Collaborate with DevOps teams to manage and troubleshoot toolchains like Docker, Kubernetes, Jenkins, Ingress Controllers etc.
  • Act as the first point of contact for technical queries and escalate issues when necessary.
  • Liaise with development and operations teams to identify root causes and resolve incidents effectively.
  • Document troubleshooting steps, solutions, and maintain a knowledge base for recurring issues.
  • Collaborate with cross-functional teams to implement best practices for monitoring and incident response.
  • Participate in shift handovers and provide timely updates on ongoing issues.

Preferred Skills

Cloud Platforms and Services

  • Hands-on knowledge working with Fargate and ECS for managing and troubleshooting containerized workloads.
  • Proficiency with DynamoDB and BigQuery for analyzing data and making decisions based on analysis.
  • Hands-on knowledge of SNS for debugging message delivery issues and integration workflows.

Monitoring and Logging Tools

  • Proficiency in CloudWatch Logs, Loki, and Splunk for consuming and analyzing logs to identify and resolve issues.
  • Hands-on knowledge with Prometheus and Grafana for analyzing metrics using dashboards and monitoring system health.
  • Knowledge of Alert Manager for configuring and managing alert escalation.
  • Ability to interpret metrics from various sources and create actionable insights.

Networking and Security

  • Understanding of load balancers (e.g., ALB, NLB) for distributing traffic and troubleshooting connectivity issues.
  • Knowledge in API Gateways like AWS API Gateway or NGINX for managing API traffic.
  • Knowledge of reverse proxies and ingress controllers (e.g., NGINX Ingress, Traefik) for managing internal/external traffic.
  • Understanding service-to-service communications, including DNS, HTTP/HTTPS, and gRPC protocols.
  • Hands-on knowledge with firewalls, security groups, and IAM roles for secure communications.
  • Troubleshooting skills for VM-related issues in platforms like AWS EC2 or equivalent.

DevOps Toolchains

  • Proficiency with Docker for managing container images and runtime debugging.
  • Understanding of Kubernetes concepts for managing deployments, ingress setups, and pod-related issues, including related troubleshooting commands and mechanisms.
  • Knowledge of CI/CD pipeline building tools such as Jenkins, GitHub Actions, ArgoCD for building, deploying, and managing automated pipelines.
  • Understanding of Ingress controllers (e.g., NGINX, Traefik) and SSL termination for secure routing.

Troubleshooting and Incident Management

  • Strong problem-solving skills to identify root causes using logs, metrics, and system-level debugging.
  • Ability to document detailed troubleshooting steps and solutions for recurring issues.

Collaboration and Communication

  • Ability to work with cross-functional teams (DevOps, development, and operations) to resolve incidents.
  • Skills in effective and proactive communication to escalate issues and provide updates during shift handovers.
  • Proficiency with tools like Slack, JIRA, Confluence, or Google Workspace for collaboration and issue tracking.

Experience: 0.5 - 2 years Salary Package: 4 - 6 LPA

Please verify the company’s legitimacy before applying. Avoid any job that asks for payment,it’s likely a scam.
